With the following codes, you are able to copy GameCube PSO 1&2 game saves from one memory card
to another.

Make Game Save Copyable [Ralf]
20385460 909C0028
C2385464 00000002
38000004 981C0034
38000000 00000000
E2000001 80008000

Make Game Save Valid [Ralf]
201FD6CC 7C040040
041FD6C8 7C0521AE
041FD6D0 4800000C
041FD76C 7C0521AE
041FD774 4800000C
E2000001 80008000

How to use these codes:

1. Save your game with the 'Make Game Save Copyable' code turned on and your source memory card
   in port A:

   To save your System file, go into the options menu from start screen and go back.
   To save your Character and Guildcard file, go ingame and quit.

2. Copy your System, Character and Guildcard file from your source memory card to your destination
   memory card (via GameCube system menu).

3. Start PSO with your destination memory card in port A and save your System file with the 'Make
   Game Save Valid' code turned on. Your game save is valid now and works fine without codes.

4. Please note that you cannot mix different game saves, because all Character and Guildcard files
   are encrypted with a unique timestamp (stored in the System file).

Character Type Modifier [Ralf]
04DDD974 00ii00jj
04DDD978 00kk00ll
02DDD97C 000000mm

ii = Costume/Body Type (00 .. 11, 00 .. 18)

jj = Skin Type (00 .. 03)
kk = Face Type (00 .. 04)
ll = Head Type (00 .. 04)
mm = Hair Type (00 .. 09)


Character Model Modifier [Ralf]
2028DC1C 7C7F1B78
0428DC20 386000xx
0428DC24 4800006C
E2000001 80008000

xx = Model ID

Bank Item Modifier Codes

Number Of Items In Bank [Ralf]
04F27EA8 000000xx

xx = Number Of Items (00 .. C8)


Weapon Modifier Codes

Bank Slot 1 Weapon Modifier [Ralf]
06F27EB0 00000018
00wwwwgg ss00iijj
kkllmmnn FFFFFFFF
00000000 00010001

Bank Slot 2 Weapon Modifier [Ralf]
06F27EC8 00000018
00wwwwgg ss00iijj
kkllmmnn FFFFFFFF
00000000 00010001

...

Bank Slot 199 Weapon Modifier [Ralf]
06F29140 00000018
00wwwwgg ss00iijj
kkllmmnn FFFFFFFF
00000000 00010001

Bank Slot 200 Weapon Modifier [Ralf]
06F29158 00000018
00wwwwgg ss00iijj
kkllmmnn FFFFFFFF
00000000 00010001

wwww = Weapon ID

gg = Weapon Grindage
ss = Weapon Special & Flags


Normal Weapons

ii = Photon Elemental Type 1
jj = Percentage Against Photon Elemental Type 1 (00 .. 7F)

kk = Photon Elemental Type 2
ll = Percentage Against Photon Elemental Type 2 (00 .. 7F)

mm = Photon Elemental Type 3
nn = Percentage Against Photon Elemental Type 3 (00 .. 7F)


S Rank Weapons

iijjkkllmmnn = Extended Weapon Name Bit Field (48 Bits)


Extended Weapon Name Bit Field

000rr0ss sssttttt 0uuuuuvv vvvwwwww 0xxxxxyy yyyzzzzz

rr = Flags

01 - Extended Weapon Name Only (No Base Weapon Name)
10 - Extended Weapon Name And Base Weapon Name

sssss = Character 1
ttttt = Character 2
uuuuu = Character 3
vvvvv = Character 4
wwwww = Character 5
xxxxx = Character 6
yyyyy = Character 7
zzzzz = Character 8

This code will let you have up to four different palettes of action buttons.


Battle Screen Control Keys

C-Stick Left  = Select Palette 1
C-Stick Down  = Select Palette 2
C-Stick Right = Select Palette 3
C-Stick Up    = Select Palette 4

Customize Menu Control Keys

C-Stick Left  = Load Palette 1 As Active Button Selection
C-Stick Down  = Load Palette 2 As Active Button Selection
C-Stick Right = Load Palette 3 As Active Button Selection
C-Stick Up    = Load Palette 4 As Active Button Selection

Hold L+R and press ...

C-Stick Left  = Save Active Button Selection As Palette 1
C-Stick Down  = Save Active Button Selection As Palette 2
C-Stick Right = Save Active Button Selection As Palette 3
C-Stick Up    = Save Active Button Selection As Palette 4

With the following codes, you are able to copy GameCube PSO 1&2 game saves from one memory card
to another.

Make Game Save Copyable [Ralf]
20385460 909C0028
C2385464 00000002
38000004 981C0034
38000000 00000000
E2000001 80008000

Make Game Save Valid [Ralf]
201FD6CC 7C040040
041FD6C8 7C0521AE
041FD6D0 4800000C
041FD76C 7C0521AE
041FD774 4800000C
E2000001 80008000

How to use these codes:

1. Save your game with the 'Make Game Save Copyable' code turned on and your source memory card
   in port A:

   To save your System file, go into the options menu from start screen and go back.
   To save your Character and Guildcard file, go ingame and quit.

2. Copy your System, Character and Guildcard file from your source memory card to your destination
   memory card (via GameCube system menu).

3. Start PSO with your destination memory card in port A and save your System file with the 'Make
   Game Save Valid' code turned on. Your game save is valid now and works fine without codes.

4. Please note that you cannot mix different game saves, because all Character and Guildcard files
   are encrypted with a unique timestamp (stored in the System file).

Extended Weapon Name Bit Field

000rr0ss sssttttt 0uuuuuvv vvvwwwww 0xxxxxyy yyyzzzzz

rr = Flags

01 - Extended Weapon Name Only (No Base Weapon Name)
10 - Extended Weapon Name And Base Weapon Name

sssss = Character 1
ttttt = Character 2
uuuuu = Character 3
vvvvv = Character 4
wwwww = Character 5
xxxxx = Character 6
yyyyy = Character 7
zzzzz = Character 8

Mag Evolution Levels Modifier [Ralf]
20112738 7FC3F378

0443E134 000000kk

ii = 1st Evolution Level (05 .. C8, Default: 0A = Level  10)
jj = 2nd Evolution Level (05 .. C8, Default: 23 = Level  35)

The 3rd evolution level must be a multiple of five and
the 4th evolution level must be a multiple of ten.

Chance Types

00 - Mag Base Chance
01 - Mag Base Chance + Synchro Boost
02 - Synchro  Boost
03 - Mag Base Chance - 10
04 - Synchro  Boost  - 10

yy = Synchro  81% - 100% Boost (00 .. 64, Default: 1E)
zz = Synchro 101% - 120% Boost (00 .. 64, Default: 23)
